# Conda example

* [PyTorch](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/PyTorch) has pip and conda installs
* [Files](https://pypi.org/project/torch/#files)

No source distribution, but built distributions for win, osx, arm and manylinux.

## Example interaction

* download wheel file for Python, suitable major.minor version and platform
* wheel contains both python files as well as packaged C++ code, e.g. ATen, ...

Running:

```
$ pip install torch-1.13.0-cp38-cp38-manylinux1_x86_64.whl
```

will collect any dependencies like `nvidia-cublas-cu11==11.10.3.66` etc. but
there is no native package or CUDA library fetched automatically.

Upon uninstallation, we see the various packages:

```
$ pip uninstall torch
Found existing installation: torch 1.13.0
Uninstalling torch-1.13.0:
  Would remove:
    ~/.virtualenvs/ta-1000/bin/convert-caffe2-to-onnx
    ~/.virtualenvs/ta-1000/bin/convert-onnx-to-caffe2
    ~/.virtualenvs/ta-1000/bin/torchrun
    ~/.virtualenvs/ta-1000/lib/python3.8/site-packages/functorch/*
    ~/.virtualenvs/ta-1000/lib/python3.8/site-packages/torch-1.13.0.dist-info/*
    ~/.virtualenvs/ta-1000/lib/python3.8/site-packages/torch/*
    ~/.virtualenvs/ta-1000/lib/python3.8/site-packages/torchgen/*
Proceed (Y/n)? y
  Successfully uninstalled torch-1.13.0
```

Example functorch:

```
$ find ~/.virtualenvs/ta-1000/lib/python3.8/site-packages/functorch/ -type f | \
    rev | cut -d . -f 1 | rev | sort | uniq -c | sort -nr

     31 pyc
     31 py
      1 so
```

That `so` depends on a couple of libraries:

```
$ ldd ~/.virtualenvs/ta-1000/lib/python3.8/site-packages/functorch/_C.cpython-38-x86_64-linux-gnu.so  | grep cublas
    libcublas.so.11 => ~/.virtualenvs/ta-1000/lib/python3.8/site-packages/functorch/../torch/lib/../../nvidia/cublas/lib/libcublas.so.11 (0x00007fccb5600000)
    libcublasLt.so.11 => ~/.virtualenvs/ta-1000/lib/python3.8/site-packages/functorch/../torch/lib/../../nvidia/cublas/lib/libcublasLt.so.11 (0x00007fcca1600000)
```

So, some more shared libraries from other python dependencies.

```
~/.virtualenvs/ta-1000/lib/python3.8/site-packages/nvidia/cublas/lib/libcublas.so.11
```

The wheel contains some dependency info:

```
$ unzip -p torch-1.13.0-cp38-cp38-manylinux1_x86_64.whl torch-1.13.0.dist-info/METADATA

Name: torch
Version: 1.13.0
Summary: Tensors and Dynamic neural networks in Python with strong GPU acceleration
Home-page: https://pytorch.org/
Author: PyTorch Team
Author-email: packages@pytorch.org
License: BSD-3
Download-URL: https://github.com/pytorch/pytorch/tags
Keywords: pytorch,machine learning
Platform: UNKNOWN
Classifier: Development Status :: 5 - Production/Stable
Classifier: Intended Audience :: Developers
Classifier: Intended Audience :: Education
Classifier: Intended Audience :: Science/Research
Classifier: License :: OSI Approved :: BSD License
Classifier: Topic :: Scientific/Engineering
Classifier: Topic :: Scientific/Engineering :: Mathematics
Classifier: Topic :: Scientific/Engineering :: Artificial Intelligence
Classifier: Topic :: Software Development
Classifier: Topic :: Software Development :: Libraries
Classifier: Topic :: Software Development :: Libraries :: Python Modules
Classifier: Programming Language :: C++
Classifier: Programming Language :: Python :: 3
Classifier: Programming Language :: Python :: 3.7
Classifier: Programming Language :: Python :: 3.8
Classifier: Programming Language :: Python :: 3.9
Classifier: Programming Language :: Python :: 3.10
Requires-Python: >=3.7.0
Description-Content-Type: text/markdown
Requires-Dist: typing-extensions
Requires-Dist: nvidia-cuda-runtime-cu11 (==11.7.99)
Requires-Dist: nvidia-cudnn-cu11 (==8.5.0.96)
Requires-Dist: nvidia-cublas-cu11 (==11.10.3.66)
Requires-Dist: nvidia-cuda-nvrtc-cu11 (==11.7.99)
...

```

* https://peps.python.org/pep-0345/#requires-dist-multiple-use

## wheel-inspect

```
$ pip install wheel-inspect
$ wheel2json torch-1.13.0-cp38-cp38-manylinux1_x86_64.whl
{
  "abi": [
    "cp38"
  ],
  "arch": [
    "manylinux1_x86_64"
  ],
  "buildver": null,
  "derived": {
    "dependencies": [
      "nvidia-cublas-cu11",
      "nvidia-cuda-nvrtc-cu11",
      "nvidia-cuda-runtime-cu11",
      "nvidia-cudnn-cu11",
      "opt-einsum",
      "typing-extensions"
    ],
    "description_in_body": true,
    "description_in_headers": false,
    "keyword_separator": ",",
    "keywords": [
      "machine learning",
      "pytorch"
    ],

...
```
